This has two terms:
1. A rational function of A: `k * A²/(a*A⁴ + 1)`
2. An exponential decay in t times A: `d * A * exp(b*t)`

Let me analyze key candidates that could potentially match.

**Candidate 7:** Contains `A**c6*c7` which could give `A²/(A⁴*c₁ + c₁)` type terms plus `A^c6` term. The first group simplifies: `A⁵*c₀*t/(A⁵*(c₁+t²))` = `c₀*t/(c₁+t²)`, etc. So the rational-in-t terms give `(c₃*t² + c₀*t + c₂)/(c₁+t²)`. Setting c₀=c₃=0 and appropriate c₂ gives a constant from that part. Then `A²*c₄/(A+c₅)²` and `A^c₆*c₇`. But there's no exp(t) term, so this can't match.

**Candidate 39:** `A²*c₀ + A*c₁*exp(c₂*t) + A*c₃ + c₄*t/(c₅+t²) + c₆*exp(A*c₇)`

The GT has `A*exp(bt)` ✓ (second term). But the first term `A²/(aA⁴+1)` is a rational function of A, not polynomial in A. `A²*c₀ + c₆*exp(A*c₇)` cannot reproduce `A²/(aA⁴+1)`. ✗

**Candidate 19:** `A²*c₀ + A*c₁ + A*c₂*exp(c₃*t) + c₄*t/(c₅+t²) + c₆*log(c₇*exp(A*c₈)+1)`

The `log(c₇*exp(A*c₈)+1)` term: for large A this is ~A*c₈, for small A it's ~log(c₇+1). This can't reproduce `A²/(aA⁴+1)`. ✗

**Candidate 9:** `[A²*c₀*t² + A²*c₂ + A*c₃*t² + A*c₄ + (c₅+c₆) + (c₇+c₉)*t² + c₈*t] / (c₁+t²)`

This equals `A²*(c₀*t²+c₂)/(c₁+t²) + A*(c₃*t²+c₄)/(c₁+t²) + ...`

The GT's A*exp(bt) term can't be represented as a rational function of t. ✗

**Candidate 25:** Similar rational-in-t structure, same problem. ✗

**Candidate 48:** Has terms like `exp(A*c₅)/(c₁+t²)` — this mixes A-dependence via exp with t-dependence rationally. The GT's first term has no t-dependence and the second has exp(t) dependence, not rational. ✗

**Candidate 18:** `A²*c₀ + A*c₁ + c₂*t/(c₃+t²) + c₄/(A+c₅) + c₆*exp(A*c₇+c₈*t)`

Setting c₂=0, c₀=0, c₁=0: `c₄/(A+c₅) + c₆*exp(A*c₇+c₈*t)`. The exp term mixes A and t — can't separate into A*exp(t) and A²/(A⁴+1). ✗

**Candidate 34:** `A*c₀*exp(c₁*t) + c₂ + c₃/A⁵`

The GT has two terms:

- Term 2: A*exp(negative*t) — exponential decay in t, linear in A
